   <xs:annotation>
      <xs:documentation xml:lang="en">Used for the European ESG Template (EET) Version 1.1.1. This update became necessary to reflect the upcoming publication in the Official Journal of the EU of the Commission Delegated Regulation amending the SFDR RTS and containing requirements for pre-contractual, periodic and website disclosure on investments in fossil gas and nuclear.</xs:documentation>
      <xs:documentation xml:lang="de">Verwendet für das European ESG Template (EET) Version 1.1.1. Dieses Update wurde notwendig, um die bevorstehende Veröffentlichung im Amtsblatt der EU der delegierten Verordnung der Kommission zur Änderung der SFDR-RTS widerzuspiegeln, die Anforderungen für vorvertragliche, periodische und Website-Offenlegungen zu Investitionen in fossiles Gas und Kernenergie enthält.</xs:documentation>
      <xs:documentation xml:lang="fr">Used pour European ESG Template (EET) Version 1.1.1. This update became necessary à reflect upcoming publication dans Official Journal de EU de Commission Delegated Regulation amending SFDR RTS et containing requirements pour pre-contractual, periodic et website disclosure on investments dans fossil gas et nuclear.</xs:documentation>
      <xs:documentation xml:lang="nl">Used voor European ESG Template (EET) Versie 1.1.1. This update became necessary naar reflect upcoming publication in Official Journal van EU van Commission Delegated Regulation amending SFDR RTS en containing requirements voor pre-contractual, periodic en website disclosure on investments in fossil gas en nuclear.</xs:documentation>
      <xs:documentation xml:lang="es">Used voor European ESG Template (EET) Versie 1.1.1. This update became necessary naar reflect upcoming publication in Official Journal van EU van Commission Delegated Regulation amending SFDR RTS en containing requirements voor pre-contractual, periodic en website disclosure on investments in fossil gas en nuclear.</xs:documentation>
      <xs:documentation xml:lang="it">Utilizzato per il modello ESG europeo (EET) versione 1.1.1. Questo aggiornamento si è reso necessario per riflettere l'imminente pubblicazione nella Gazzetta Ufficiale dell'UE del Regolamento Delegato della Commissione che modifica la SFDR RTS e contiene requisiti per l'informativa precontrattuale, periodica e web sugli investimenti nel gas fossile e nel nucleare.</xs:documentation>
      <xs:documentation xml:lang="cs">Použito pro the European ESG Template (EET) Version 1.1.1. This update became necessary to reflect the upcoming publication in the Official Journal of the EU of the Commission Delegated Regulation amending the SFDR RTS and containing requirements for pre-contractual, periodic and website disclosure on investments in fossil gas and nuclear.</xs:documentation>
      <xs:documentation xml:lang="hu">Hasznalt for the Europai ESG Sablon (EET) Verzio 1.1.1. This update became necessary to reflect the upcoming Kozzetétel in the Official Journal of the EU of the Commission Felhatalmazason alapulo Regulation amending the SFDR RTS and containing requirements for pre-contractual, periodic and website disclosure on investments in fosszilis gas and nuclear.</xs:documentation>

                  <xs:annotation>
                     <xs:documentation xml:lang="en">20000_Financial_Instrument_Identifying_Data
Use the following priority:
  - ISO 6166 code of ISIN when available
  - Other recognised codes (e.g.: CUSIP, Bloomberg Ticker, Reuters RIC)

               <xs:element name="TypeOfIdentification">
                  <xs:annotation>
                     <xs:documentation xml:lang="en">20010_Financial_Instrument_Type_Of_Identification_Code
One of the options in the following closed list to be used:
1 - ISO 6166 for ISIN code
2 - CUSIP (The Committee on Uniform Securities Identification Procedures number assigned by the CUSIP Service Bureau for U.S. and Canadian companies)
3 - SEDOL (Stock Exchange Daily Official List for the London Stock Exchange)
4 – WKN (Wertpapier Kenn-Nummer, the alphanumeric German identification number)
5 - Bloomberg Ticker (Bloomberg letters code that identify a company's securities)
6 - BBGID (The Bloomberg Global ID)
7 - Reuters RIC (Reuters instrument code)
